I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
ForEachItem task delayed/stuck RUNNING after all child subflows complete including afterExecution
## Description:

When using the **io.kestra.plugin.core.flow.ForEachItem** task  to execute a large number of child subflows, the ForEachItem task itself remains in a RUNNING state for an extended period after all spawned child subflow executions, **including their afterExecution blocks**, have successfully completed and reached a final status in the Kestra UI. 
 
 
 
## Steps to Reproduce:

- Define two flows: a parent flow and a subflow, as provided below.
- The parent flow uses ForEachItem to iterate a number of items
- The ForEachItem task is configured with wait: true, batch.rows: 1, and calls the defined subflow.
- The subflow contains simple tasks (e.g., Log) and importantly, includes an afterExecution block.
- The parent flow has a task defined after the ForEachItem task.
 
 
 
## Expected behavior:

The ForEachItem task should transition from RUNNING to a final state shortly after the last child execution it was waiting for ts afterExecution phase completes. 

## Observed behavior:

The ForEachItem task in the parent flow remains in the RUNNING state for a considerable amount of time after all 1000 child subflow executions are confirmed as SUCCESS in the UI. This includes confirmation that the afterExecution task ran and completed for all child subflows. 

## Minimal Reproducible Example:

### Parent Flow:

```yaml
id: flow
namespace: test.flow

tasks:
  - id: extract
    type: io.kestra.plugin.jdbc.duckdb.Query
    sql: |
      INSTALL httpfs;
      LOAD httpfs;
      SELECT *
      FROM read_csv_auto('https://huggingface.co/datasets/kestra/datasets/raw/main/csv/orders.csv', header=True);
    store: true
  - id: each
    type: io.kestra.plugin.core.flow.ForEachItem
    items: "{{ outputs.extract.uri }}"
    batch:
      rows: 1
    namespace: test.flow
    flowId: subflow
    wait: true # wait for the subflow execution (including its afterExecution)
    transmitFailed: true # fail the task run if the subflow execution fails
    inputs:
      order: "{{ taskrun.items }}"
  - id: hello 
    type: io.kestra.plugin.core.log.Log
    message: Hello World!
```

### Sub Flow:

```yaml
id: subflow
namespace: test.flow

tasks:
  - id: hello
    type: io.kestra.plugin.core.log.Log
    message: Hello World! 🚀

afterExecution:
  - id: hello21
    type: io.kestra.plugin.core.log.Log
    message: Hello from afterExecution!
```

### Environment

Kestra Version: 0.22.4
OS: Linux
Executions, stuck in QUEUED state due to concurrency, never finish
### Describe the issue

Hello,

I am experiencing issues with flow concurrency. I use QUEUE mechanism for concurrency but it doesn't seem to work properly. All the executions that were put in QUEUED state due to concurrent multiple concurrent executions, will stuck in it forever and never finish. Here is yaml of such workflow:

```

namespace: default
inputs:

        runIf: "{{ json(outputs.task_27_1000017_request.body).process ?? true }}"

          type: io.kestra.plugin.scripts.runner.docker.Docker

        script: |-
          import yaml

          from kestra import Kestra
          import csv

          definition1_url = '{{inputs.definice_soubor ?? null}}'

          def evaluate_expression(expression, row):
              # expression is list, evaluate as function
              if isinstance(expression, list):
                  func, args = expression[0], expression[1:]
                  # evaluate function
                  match (func):
                      case '+':
                          return reduce(lambda x, y: (x + y) if x is not None and y is not None else x, [evaluate_expression(arg, element) for arg in args])
                      case '-':
                          return reduce(lambda x, y: (x - y) if x is not None and y is not None else x, [evaluate_expression(arg, element) for arg in args])
                      case '*':
                          return reduce(lambda x, y: (x * y) if x is not None and y is not None else x, [evaluate_expression(arg, element) for arg in args])
                      case '/':
                          return reduce(lambda x, y: (x / y) if x is not None and y is not None and y != 0 else x, [evaluate_expression(arg, element) for arg in args])
                      case "concat":
                          return ''.join([str(evaluate_expression(arg, element)) for arg in args])
              else:
                  # extract value from row if wrapped in $()
                  if isinstance(expression, str) and expression.startswith('$('):
                      column = re.findall(r'\$\((\w+)\)', expression)[0]
                      if column is None:
                          return column
                      return row.get(column)
                  else:
                      return eval(expression, {'__builtins__': {}})
          with open(definition1_url, 'r') as input_file:
              with open(output_url, 'w') as output_file:
                  with open(input_url, 'r') as file:
                      definition = yaml.safe_load(input_file)
                      mappings = definition['SPECIFIKACE_POLOZEK']
                      if mappings is None:
                          raise Exception('Specifikace polozek je prazdna')
                      index = 0
                      for row in csv.DictReader(file):
                          row_data = {}
                          for key, expression in mappings.items():
                              if index == 0:
                                  headers.append(key)
                              row_data[key] = evaluate_expression(expression, row)
                          output_file.write(simpleion.dumps(row_data, binary=False, omit_version_marker=True) + '\n')
                          index += 1
          Kestra.outputs({ 'hlavicka': ','.join(headers), 'insert_vyraz': ','.join(len(headers) * ['?']) })
afterExecution:
- id: post_request
  type: io.kestra.plugin.core.http.Request
  uri: "{{ envs.api_public_url }}/api/processing/6/execution/{{ execution.id }}/finished"
```

    58	    title = "Execute a subflow for each batch of items",
    59	    description = """
    60	        The `items` value must be Kestra's internal storage URI e.g. an output file from a previous task, or a file from inputs of FILE type.
    61	        Two special variables are available to pass as inputs to the subflow:
    62	        - `taskrun.items` which is the URI of internal storage file containing the batch of items to process
    63	        - `taskrun.iteration` which is the iteration or batch number
    64	
    65	        Restarting a parent flow will restart any subflows that has previously been executed."""

   123	                Execute a subflow for each JSON item fetched from a REST API. The subflow `mysubflow` is called from the parent flow `iterate_over_json` using the `ForEachItem` task; this creates one subflow execution for each JSON object.
   124	
   125	                Note how we first need to convert the JSON array to JSON-L format using the `JsonWriter` task. This is because the `items` attribute of the `ForEachItem` task expects a file where each line represents a single item. Suitable file types include Amazon ION (commonly produced by Query tasks), newline-separated JSON files, or CSV files formatted with one row per line and without a header. For other formats, you can use the conversion tasks available in the `io.kestra.plugin.serdes` module.
   126	
   127	                In this example, the subflow `mysubflow` expects a JSON object as input. The `JsonReader` task first reads the JSON array from the REST API and converts it to ION. Then, the `JsonWriter` task converts that ION file to JSON-L format, suitable for the `ForEachItem` task.
   128

   235	public class ForEachItem extends Task implements FlowableTask<VoidOutput>, ChildFlowInterface {
   236	    @NotEmpty
   237	    @PluginProperty(dynamic = true)
   238	    @Schema(title = "The items to be split into batches and processed. Make sure to set it to Kestra's internal storage URI. This can be either the output from a previous task, formatted as `{{ outputs.task_id.uri }}`, or a FILE type input parameter, like `{{ inputs.myfile }}`. This task is optimized for files where each line represents a single item. Suitable file types include Amazon ION-type files (commonly produced by Query tasks), newline-separated JSON files, or CSV files formatted with one row per line and without a header. For files in other formats such as Excel, CSV, Avro, Parquet, XML, or JSON, it's recommended to first convert them to the ION format. This can be done using the conversion tasks available in the `io.kestra.plugin.serdes` module, which will transform files from their original format to ION.")
   239	    private String items;
   240	
   241	    @NotNull
   242	    @PluginProperty
   243	    @Builder.Default

   245	    private ForEachItem.Batch batch = Batch.builder().build();

   303	    @PluginProperty

   322	    }

   331	    @NotNull
   332	    @Builder.Default

   334	
   335	    @Override
   336	    public GraphCluster tasksTree(Execution execution, TaskRun taskRun, List<String> parentValues) throws IllegalVariableEvaluationException {
   337	        GraphCluster subGraph = new GraphCluster(this, taskRun, parentValues, RelationType.SEQUENTIAL);
   338	
   339	        GraphUtils.sequential(
   340	            subGraph,
   341	            this.getTasks(),
   342	            this.errors,
   343	            this._finally,
   344	            taskRun,
   345	            execution
   346	        );
   347	
   348	        return subGraph;
   349	    }
   350	
   351	    @Override
   352	    public List<Task> allChildTasks() {
   353	        return Stream
   354	            .concat(
   355	                this.getTasks() != null ? this.getTasks().stream() : Stream.empty(),
   356	                Stream.concat(
   357	                    this.errors != null ? this.errors.stream() : Stream.empty(),
   358	                    this._finally != null ? this._finally.stream() : Stream.empty()
   359	                )
   360	            )
   361	            .toList();
   362	    }
   363	
   364	    @Override
   365	    public List<ResolvedTask> childTasks(RunContext runContext, TaskRun parentTaskRun) throws IllegalVariableEvaluationException {
   366	        return FlowableUtils.resolveTasks(this.getTasks(), parentTaskRun);
   367	    }
   368	
   369	    @Override
   370	    public List<NextTaskRun> resolveNexts(RunContext runContext, Execution execution, TaskRun parentTaskRun) throws IllegalVariableEvaluationException {
   371	        return FlowableUtils.resolveSequentialNexts(
   372	            execution,
   373	            this.childTasks(runContext, parentTaskRun),
   374	            FlowableUtils.resolveTasks(this.errors, parentTaskRun),
   375	            FlowableUtils.resolveTasks(this._finally, parentTaskRun),
   376	            parentTaskRun
   377	        );
   378	    }

   483	                return splits
   484	                    .stream()
   485	                    .map(throwFunction(
   486	                        split -> {
   487	                            int iteration = currentIteration.getAndIncrement();
   488	                            // these are special variable that can be passed to the subflow
   489	                            Map<String, Object> itemsVariable = Map.of("taskrun",
   490	                                Map.of("items", split, "iteration", iteration));
   491	                            Map<String, Object> inputs = new HashMap<>();
   492	                            if (this.inputs != null) {
   493	                                inputs.putAll(runContext.render(this.inputs, itemsVariable));
   494	                            }
   495	
   496	                            // these are special outputs to be able to compute the iteration map of the parent taskrun
   497	                            var outputs = Output.builder()
   498	                                .numberOfBatches(splits.size())
   499	                                // the passed URI may be used by the subflow to write execution outputs.
   500	                                .uri(URI.create(runContext.getStorageOutputPrefix().toString() + "/" + iteration + "/outputs.ion"))
   501	                                .build();
   502	
   503	                                return ExecutableUtils.subflowExecution(
   504	                                    runContext,
   505	                                    flowExecutorInterface,
   506	                                    currentExecution,
   507	                                    currentFlow,
   508	                                    this,
   509	                                    currentTaskRun
   510	                                        .withOutputs(Variables.inMemory(outputs.toMap()))
   511	                                        .withIteration(iteration),
   512	                                    inputs,
   513	                                    labels,
   514	                                    inheritLabels,
   515	                                    scheduleOn
   516	                                );
   517	                        }
   518	                    ))
   519	                    .filter(Optional::isPresent)
   520	                    .<SubflowExecution<?>>map(Optional::get)
   521	                    .toList();
   522	            } catch (IOException e) {
   523	                throw new InternalException(e);
   524	            }
   525	        }
   526	
   527	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   528	        @Override
   529	        public Optional<SubflowExecutionResult> createSubflowExecutionResult(
   530	            RunContext runContext,
   531	            TaskRun taskRun,
   532	            FlowInterface flow,
   533	            Execution execution
   534	        ) {
   535	
   536	            // We only resolve subflow outputs for an execution result when the execution is terminated.
   537	            if (taskRun.getState().isTerminated() && flow.getOutputs() != null && waitForExecution()) {
   538	                final Map<String, Object> outputs = flow.getOutputs()
   539	                    .stream()
   540	                    .collect(Collectors.toMap(
   541	                        io.kestra.core.models.flows.Output::getId,
   542	                        io.kestra.core.models.flows.Output::getValue)
   543	                    );
   544	                final ForEachItem.Output.OutputBuilder builder = Output
   545	                    .builder()
   546	                    .iterations((Map<State.Type, Integer>) taskRun.getOutputs().get(ExecutableUtils.TASK_VARIABLE_ITERATIONS))
   547	                    .numberOfBatches((Integer) taskRun.getOutputs().get(ExecutableUtils.TASK_VARIABLE_NUMBER_OF_BATCHES));
   548	
   549	                try (ByteArrayOutputStream bos = new ByteArrayOutputStream()) {
   550	                    FileSerde.write(bos, runContext.render(outputs));
   551	                    URI uri = runContext.storage().putFile(
   552	                        new ByteArrayInputStream(bos.toByteArray()),
   553	                        URI.create((String) taskRun.getOutputs().get("uri"))
   554	                    );
   555	                    builder.uri(uri);
   556	                } catch (Exception e) {
   557	                    runContext.logger().warn("Failed to extract outputs with the error: '{}'", e.getLocalizedMessage(), e);
   558	                    var state = State.Type.fail(this);
   559	                    taskRun = taskRun
   560	                        .withState(state)
   561	                        .withAttempts(Collections.singletonList(TaskRunAttempt.builder().state(new State().withState(state)).build()))
   562	                        .withOutputs(Variables.inMemory(builder.build().toMap()));
   563	
   564	                    return Optional.of(SubflowExecutionResult.builder()
   565	                        .executionId(execution.getId())
   566	                        .state(State.Type.FAILED)
   567	                        .parentTaskRun(taskRun)
   568	                        .build());
   569	                }
   570	                taskRun = taskRun.withOutputs(Variables.inMemory(builder.build().toMap()));
   571	            }
   572	
   573	            // ForEachItem is an iterative task, the terminal state will be computed in the executor while counting on the task run execution list
   574	            return Optional.of(ExecutableUtils.subflowExecutionResult(taskRun, execution));
   575	        }
   576	
   577	        @Override
   578	        public boolean waitForExecution() {
   579	            return this.wait;
   580	        }
   581	
   582	        @Override
   583	        public SubflowId subflowId() {
   584	            return this.subflowId;
   585	        }
   586	    }
   587	
   588	    @Plugin(internal = true)
   589	    @Getter
   590	    @NoArgsConstructor
   591	    public static class ForEachItemMergeOutputs extends Task implements RunnableTask<ForEachItemMergeOutputs.Output> {
   592	        static final String SUFFIX = "_merge";
   593	
   594	        private ForEachItemMergeOutputs(String parentId) {
   595	            this.id = parentId + SUFFIX;
   596	            this.type = ForEachItemMergeOutputs.class.getName();
   597	        }
   598	
   599	        @Override
   600	        public ForEachItemMergeOutputs.Output run(RunContext runContext) throws Exception {
   601	            // get the list of splits from the outputs of the split task
   602	            String taskId = this.id.substring(0, this.id.lastIndexOf('_')) + ForEachItemExecutable.SUFFIX;
   603	            var taskOutput = extractOutput(runContext, taskId);
   604	            if (taskOutput == null) {
   605	                // there were no subflow executions
   606	                return null;
   607	            }
   608	
   609	            String subflowOutputsBase = (String) taskOutput.get(ExecutableUtils.TASK_VARIABLE_SUBFLOW_OUTPUTS_BASE_URI);
   610	            URI subflowOutputsBaseUri = URI.create(StorageContext.KESTRA_PROTOCOL + subflowOutputsBase + "/");
   611	
   612	            StorageInterface storage = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(StorageInterface.class);
   613	            if (storage.exists(runContext.flowInfo().tenantId(), runContext.flowInfo().namespace(), subflowOutputsBaseUri)) {
   614	                List<FileAttributes> list = storage.list(runContext.flowInfo().tenantId(), runContext.flowInfo().namespace(), subflowOutputsBaseUri);
   615	
   616	                if (!list.isEmpty()) {
   617	                    // Merge outputs from each sub-flow into a single stored in the internal storage.
   618	                    List<InputStream> streams = list.stream()
   619	                        .map(throwFunction(attr -> {
   620	                            URI file = subflowOutputsBaseUri.resolve(attr.getFileName() + "/outputs.ion");
   621	                            return runContext.storage().getFile(file);
   622	                        }))
   623	                        .toList();
   624	                    try (InputStream is = new SequenceInputStream(Collections.enumeration(streams))) {
   625	                        URI uri = runContext.storage().putFile(is, "outputs.ion");
   626	                        return ForEachItemMergeOutputs.Output.builder().subflowOutputs(uri).build();
   627	                    }
   628	                }
   629	            }
   630	
   631	            return null;
   632	        }
   633	
   634	        @Builder
   635	        @Getter
   636	        public static class Output implements io.kestra.core.models.tasks.Output {
   637	            private URI subflowOutputs;
   638	        }
   639	    }

    47	    public static State.Type guessState(Execution execution, boolean transmitFailed, boolean allowedFailure, boolean allowWarning) {
    48	        if (transmitFailed &&
    49	            (execution.getState().isFailed() || execution.getState().isPaused() || execution.getState().getCurrent() == State.Type.KILLED || execution.getState().getCurrent() == State.Type.WARNING)
    50	        ) {
    51	            State.Type finalState = (allowedFailure && execution.getState().isFailed()) ? State.Type.WARNING : execution.getState().getCurrent();
    52	            return finalState.equals(State.Type.WARNING) && allowWarning ? State.Type.SUCCESS : finalState;
    53	        } else {
    54	            return State.Type.SUCCESS;
    55	        }
    56	    }

    58	    public static SubflowExecutionResult subflowExecutionResult(TaskRun parentTaskrun, Execution execution) {
    59	        List<TaskRunAttempt> attempts = parentTaskrun.getAttempts() == null ? new ArrayList<>() : new ArrayList<>(parentTaskrun.getAttempts());
    60	        attempts.add(TaskRunAttempt.builder().state(parentTaskrun.getState()).build());
    61	        return SubflowExecutionResult.builder()
    62	            .executionId(execution.getId())
    63	            .state(parentTaskrun.getState().getCurrent())
    64	            .parentTaskRun(parentTaskrun.withAttempts(attempts))
    65	            .build();
    66	    }

    68	    public static <T extends Task & ExecutableTask<?>> Optional<SubflowExecution<?>> subflowExecution(
    69	        RunContext runContext,
    70	        FlowMetaStoreInterface flowExecutorInterface,
    71	        Execution currentExecution,
    72	        Flow currentFlow,
    73	        T currentTask,
    74	        TaskRun currentTaskRun,
    75	        Map<String, Object> inputs,
    76	        List<Label> labels,
    77	        boolean inheritLabels,
    78	        Property<ZonedDateTime> scheduleDate
    79	    ) throws IllegalVariableEvaluationException {
    80	
    81	        // extract a trace context for propagation
    82	        final Optional<TextMapPropagator> propagator = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext()
    83	            .findBean(OpenTelemetry.class)
    84	            .map(OpenTelemetry::getPropagators)
    85	            .map(ContextPropagators::getTextMapPropagator);
    86	
    87	        var tracerFactory = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(TracerFactory.class);
    88	        var tracer = tracerFactory.getTracer(currentTask.getClass(), "EXECUTOR");
    89	
    90	        return tracer.inNewContext(
    91	            currentExecution,
    92	            currentTask.getType(),
    93	            throwCallable(() -> {
    94	            // If we are in a flow that is restarted, we search for existing run of the task to restart them
    95	            if (currentExecution.getLabels() != null && currentExecution.getLabels().contains(new Label(Label.RESTARTED, "true"))
    96	                && currentTask.getRestartBehavior() == ExecutableTask.RestartBehavior.RETRY_FAILED) {
    97	                ExecutionRepositoryInterface executionRepository = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(ExecutionRepositoryInterface.class);
    98	
    99	                Optional<Execution> existingSubflowExecution = Optional.empty();
   100	                if (currentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null && currentTaskRun.getOutputs().containsKey("executionId")) {
   101	                    // we know which execution to restart; this should be the case for Subflow tasks
   102	                    existingSubflowExecution = executionRepository.findById(currentExecution.getTenantId(), (String) currentTaskRun.getOutputs().get("executionId"));
   103	                }
   104	
   105	                if (existingSubflowExecution.isEmpty()) {
   106	                    // otherwise, we try to find the correct one; this should be the case for ForEachItem tasks
   107	                    List<Execution> childExecutions = executionRepository.findAllByTriggerExecutionId(currentExecution.getTenantId(), currentExecution.getId())
   108	                        .filter(e -> e.getNamespace().equals(currentTask.subflowId().namespace()) && e.getFlowId().equals(currentTask.subflowId().flowId()) && e.getTrigger().getId().equals(currentTask.getId()))
   109	                        .filter(e -> Objects.equals(e.getTrigger().getVariables().get("taskRunId"), currentTaskRun.getId()) && Objects.equals(e.getTrigger().getVariables().get("taskRunValue"), currentTaskRun.getValue()) && Objects.equals(e.getTrigger().getVariables().get("taskRunIteration"), currentTaskRun.getIteration()))
   110	                        .collectList()
   111	                        .block();
   112	
   113	                    if (childExecutions != null && childExecutions.size() == 1) {
   114	                        // if there are more than one, we ignore the results and create a new one
   115	                        existingSubflowExecution = Optional.of(childExecutions.getFirst());
   116	                    }
   117	                }
   118	
   119	                if (existingSubflowExecution.isPresent()) {
   120	                    Execution subflowExecution = existingSubflowExecution.get();
   121	                    if (!subflowExecution.getState().isFailed()) {
   122	                        // don't restart it as it's terminated successfully
   123	                        return Optional.empty();
   124	                    }
   125	                    ExecutionService executionService = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(ExecutionService.class);
   126	                    try {
   127	                        Execution restarted = executionService.restart(subflowExecution, null);
   128	
   129	                        // inject the traceparent into the new execution
   130	                        propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), restarted, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));
   131	
   132	                        return Optional.of(SubflowExecution.builder()
   133	                            .parentTask(currentTask)
   134	                            .parentTaskRun(currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING))
   135	                            .execution(restarted)
   136	                            .build());
   137	                    } catch (Exception e) {
   138	                        throw new RuntimeException(e);
   139	                    }
   140	                }
   141	            }
   142	
   143	            String subflowNamespace = runContext.render(currentTask.subflowId().namespace());
   144	            String subflowId = runContext.render(currentTask.subflowId().flowId());
   145	            Optional<Integer> subflowRevision = currentTask.subflowId().revision();
   146	
   147	            FlowInterface flow = flowExecutorInterface.findByIdFromTask(
   148	                    currentExecution.getTenantId(),
   149	                    subflowNamespace,
   150	                    subflowId,
   151	                    subflowRevision,
   152	                    currentExecution.getTenantId(),
   153	                    currentFlow.getNamespace(),
   154	                    currentFlow.getId()
   155	                )
   156	                .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Unable to find flow '" + subflowNamespace + "'.'" + subflowId + "' with revision '" + subflowRevision.orElse(0) + "'"));
   157	
   158	            if (flow.isDisabled()) {
   159	                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot execute a flow which is disabled");
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            if (flow instanceof FlowWithException fwe) {
   163	                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot execute an invalid flow: " + fwe.getException());
   164	            }
   165	
   166	            List<Label> newLabels = inheritLabels ? new ArrayList<>(filterLabels(currentExecution.getLabels(), flow)) : new ArrayList<>(systemLabels(currentExecution));
   167	            if (labels != null) {
   168	                labels.forEach(throwConsumer(label -> newLabels.add(new Label(runContext.render(label.key()), runContext.render(label.value())))));
   169	            }
   170	
   171	            var variables = ImmutableMap.<String, Object>builder().putAll(Map.of(
   172	                "executionId", currentExecution.getId(),
   173	                "namespace", currentFlow.getNamespace(),
   174	                "flowId", currentFlow.getId(),
   175	                "flowRevision", currentFlow.getRevision(),
   176	                "taskRunId", currentTaskRun.getId(),
   177	                "taskId", currentTaskRun.getTaskId()
   178	            ));
   179	            if (currentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null) {
   180	                variables.put("taskRunOutputs", currentTaskRun.getOutputs());
   181	            }
   182	            if (currentTaskRun.getValue() != null) {
   183	                variables.put("taskRunValue", currentTaskRun.getValue());
   184	            }
   185	            if (currentTaskRun.getIteration() != null) {
   186	                variables.put("taskRunIteration", currentTaskRun.getIteration());
   187	            }
   188	
   189	            FlowInputOutput flowInputOutput = ((DefaultRunContext)runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(FlowInputOutput.class);
   190	            Instant scheduleOnDate = runContext.render(scheduleDate).as(ZonedDateTime.class).map(date -> date.toInstant()).orElse(null);
   191	            Execution execution = Execution
   192	                .newExecution(
   193	                    flow,
   194	                    (f, e) -> flowInputOutput.readExecutionInputs(f, e, inputs),
   195	                    newLabels,
   196	                    Optional.empty())
   197	                .withTrigger(ExecutionTrigger.builder()
   198	                    .id(currentTask.getId())
   199	                    .type(currentTask.getType())
   200	                    .variables(variables.build())
   201	                    .build()
   202	                )
   203	                .withScheduleDate(scheduleOnDate);
   204	
   205	            // inject the traceparent into the new execution
   206	            propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), execution, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));
   207	
   208	            return Optional.of(SubflowExecution.builder()
   209	                .parentTask(currentTask)
   210	                .parentTaskRun(currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING))
   211	                .execution(execution)
   212	                .build());
   213	        }));
   214	    }
   215	
   216	    private static List<Label> filterLabels(List<Label> labels, FlowInterface flow) {
   217	        if (ListUtils.isEmpty(flow.getLabels())) {
   218	            return labels;
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        return labels.stream()
   222	            .filter(label -> flow.getLabels().stream().noneMatch(flowLabel -> flowLabel.key().equals(label.key())))
   223	            .toList();
   224	    }
   225	
   226	    private static List<Label> systemLabels(Execution execution) {
   227	        return Streams.of(execution.getLabels())
   228	            .filter(label -> label.key().startsWith(Label.SYSTEM_PREFIX))
   229	            .toList();
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   233	    public static TaskRun manageIterations(Storage storage, TaskRun taskRun, Execution execution, boolean transmitFailed, boolean allowFailure, boolean allowWarning) throws InternalException {
   234	        Integer numberOfBatches = (Integer) taskRun.getOutputs().get(TASK_VARIABLE_NUMBER_OF_BATCHES);
   235	        var previousTaskRun = execution.findTaskRunByTaskRunId(taskRun.getId());
   236	        if (previousTaskRun == null) {
   237	            throw new IllegalStateException("Should never happen");
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        State.Type currentState = taskRun.getState().getCurrent();
   241	        Optional<State.Type> previousState = taskRun.getState().getHistories().size() > 1 ?
   242	            Optional.of(taskRun.getState().getHistories().get(taskRun.getState().getHistories().size() - 2).getState()) :
   243	            Optional.empty();
   244	
   245	        // search for the previous iterations, if not found, we init it with an empty map
   246	        Map<String, Integer> iterations = !MapUtils.isEmpty(previousTaskRun.getOutputs()) ?
   247	            (Map<String, Integer>) previousTaskRun.getOutputs().get(TASK_VARIABLE_ITERATIONS) :
   248	            new HashMap<>();
   249	
   250	        int currentStateIteration = iterations.getOrDefault(currentState.toString(), 0);
   251	        iterations.put(currentState.toString(), currentStateIteration + 1);
   252	        if (previousState.isPresent() && previousState.get() != currentState) {
   253	            int previousStateIterations = iterations.getOrDefault(previousState.get().toString(), numberOfBatches);
   254	            iterations.put(previousState.get().toString(), previousStateIterations - 1);
   255	
   256	            if (previousState.get() == State.Type.RESTARTED) {
   257	                // if we are in a restart, we need to reset the failed executions
   258	                iterations.put(State.Type.FAILED.toString(), 0);
   259	            }
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        // update the state to success if terminatedIterations == numberOfBatches
   263	        int terminatedIterations = iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.SUCCESS.toString(), 0) +
   264	            iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.FAILED.toString(), 0) +
   265	            iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.KILLED.toString(), 0) +
   266	            iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.WARNING.toString(), 0) +
   267	            iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.CANCELLED.toString(), 0);
   268	
   269	        if (terminatedIterations == numberOfBatches) {
   270	            State.Type state = transmitFailed ? findTerminalState(iterations, allowFailure, allowWarning) : State.Type.SUCCESS;
   271	            final Map<String, Object> outputs = new HashMap<>();
   272	            outputs.put(TASK_VARIABLE_ITERATIONS, iterations);
   273	            outputs.put(TASK_VARIABLE_NUMBER_OF_BATCHES, numberOfBatches);
   274	            outputs.put(TASK_VARIABLE_SUBFLOW_OUTPUTS_BASE_URI, storage.getContextBaseURI().getPath());
   275	
   276	            return previousTaskRun
   277	                .withIteration(taskRun.getIteration())
   278	                .withOutputs(Variables.inMemory(outputs))
   279	                .withAttempts(Collections.singletonList(TaskRunAttempt.builder().state(new State().withState(state)).build()))
   280	                .withState(state);
   281	        }
   282	
   283	        // else we update the previous taskRun as it's the same taskRun that is still running
   284	        return previousTaskRun
   285	            .withIteration(taskRun.getIteration())
   286	            .withOutputs(Variables.inMemory(Map.of(
   287	                TASK_VARIABLE_ITERATIONS, iterations,
   288	                TASK_VARIABLE_NUMBER_OF_BATCHES, numberOfBatches
   289	            )));
   290	    }
   291	
   292	    private static State.Type findTerminalState(Map<String, Integer> iterations, boolean allowFailure, boolean allowWarning) {
   293	        if (iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.FAILED.toString(), 0) > 0) {
   294	            return allowFailure ? allowWarning ? State.Type.SUCCESS : State.Type.WARNING : State.Type.FAILED;
   295	        }
   296	        if (iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.KILLED.toString(), 0) > 0) {
   297	            return State.Type.KILLED;
   298	        }
   299	        if (iterations.getOrDefault(State.Type.WARNING.toString(), 0) > 0) {
   300	         <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

    96	    protected FlowMetaStoreInterface flowExecutorInterface() {
    97	        // bean is injected late, so we need to wait
    98	        if (this.flowExecutorInterface == null) {
    99	            this.flowExecutorInterface = applicationContext.getBean(FlowMetaStoreInterface.class);
   100	        }

   104	
   105	    public ExecutionRunning processExecutionRunning(FlowInterface flow, int runningCount, ExecutionRunning executionRunning) {
   106	        // if concurrency was removed, it can be null as we always get the latest flow definition
   107	        if (flow.getConcurrency() != null && runningCount >= flow.getConcurrency().getLimit()) {
   108	            return switch (flow.getConcurrency().getBehavior()) {
   109	                case QUEUE -> {
   110	                    logService.logExecution(
   111	                        executionRunning.getExecution(),
   112	                        Level.INFO,
   113	                        "Execution is queued due to concurrency limit exceeded, {} running(s)",
   114	                        runningCount
   115	                    );
   116	                    var newExecution = executionRunning.getExecution().withState(State.Type.QUEUED);
   117	                    metricRegistry.counter(MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_EXECUTION_QUEUED_COUNT, MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_EXECUTION_QUEUED_COUNT_DESCRIPTION, metricRegistry.tags(newExecution)).increment();
   118	                    yield executionRunning
   119	                        .withExecution(newExecution)
   120	                        .withConcurrencyState(ExecutionRunning.ConcurrencyState.QUEUED);
   121	                }
   122	                case CANCEL ->
   123	                    executionRunning
   124	                        .withExecution(executionRunning.getExecution().withState(State.Type.CANCELLED))
   125	                        .withConcurrencyState(ExecutionRunning.ConcurrencyState.RUNNING);
   126	                case FAIL ->
   127	                    executionRunning
   128	                        .withExecution(executionRunning.getExecution().failedExecutionFromExecutor(new IllegalStateException("Execution is FAILED due to concurrency limit exceeded")).getExecution())
   129	                        .withConcurrencyState(ExecutionRunning.ConcurrencyState.RUNNING);
   130	
   131	            };
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        // if under the limit, run it!
   135	        return executionRunning
   136	            .withExecution(executionRunning.getExecution().withState(State.Type.RUNNING))
   137	            .withConcurrencyState(ExecutionRunning.ConcurrencyState.RUNNING);
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    public Executor process(Executor executor) {
   141	        // previous failed (flow join can fail), just forward
   142	        // or concurrency limit failed/cancelled the execution
   143	        if (!executor.canBeProcessed() || executionService.isTerminated(executor.getFlow(), executor.getExecution())) {
   144	            return executor;
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        long nanos = System.nanoTime();
   148	        try {
   149	            executor = this.handleRestart(executor);
   150	            executor = this.handleEnd(executor);
   151	            // if killing: move created tasks to killed as they are not already started
   152	            executor = this.handleCreatedKilling(executor);
   153	            //then set the execution to killed
   154	            executor = this.handleKilling(executor);
   155	
   156	            // process next task if not killing or killed
   157	            if (executor.getExecution().getState().getCurrent() != State.Type.KILLING && executor.getExecution().getState().getCurrent() != State.Type.KILLED && executor.getExecution().getState().getCurrent() != State.Type.QUEUED) {
   158	                executor = this.handleNext(executor);
   159	                executor = this.handleChildNext(executor);
   160	            }
   161	
   162	            // but keep listeners on killing
   163	            executor = this.handleAfterExecution(executor);
   164	
   165	            // search for worker task
   166	            executor = this.handleWorkerTask(executor);
   167	
   168	            // search for worker task result
   169	            executor = this.handleChildWorkerTaskResult(executor);
   170	
   171	            // search for execution updating tasks
   172	            executor = this.handleExecutionUpdatingTask(executor);
   173	
   174	            // search for flow task
   175	            executor = this.handleExecutableTask(executor);
   176	        } catch (Exception e) {
   177	            return executor.withException(e, "process");
   178	        } finally {
   179	            metricRegistry
   180	                .timer(MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_EXECUTION_MESSAGE_PROCESS_DURATION, MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_EXECUTION_MESSAGE_PROCESS_DURATION_DESCRIPTION, metricRegistry.tags(executor.getExecution()))
   181	                .record(Duration.ofNanos(System.nanoTime() - nanos));
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        return executor;
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    public Execution onNexts(Execution execution, List<TaskRun> nexts) {
   188	        if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {
   189	            logService.logExecution(
   190	                execution,
   191	                Level.TRACE,
   192	                "Found {} next(s) {}",
   193	                nexts.size(),
   194	                nexts
   195	            );
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        List<TaskRun> executionTasksRun;
   199	        Execution newExecution;
   200	
   201	        if (execution.getTaskRunList() == null) {
   202	            executionTasksRun = nexts;
   203	        } else {
   204	            executionTasksRun = new ArrayList<>(execution.getTaskRunList());
   205	            executionTasksRun.addAll(nexts);
   206	        }
   207	
   208	        // update Execution
   209	        newExecution = execution.withTaskRunList(executionTasksRun);
   210	
   211	        if (execution.getState().getCurrent() == State.Type.CREATED) {
   212	            metricRegistry
   213	                .counter(MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_EXECUTION_STARTED_COUNT, MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_EXECUTION_STARTED_COUNT_DESCRIPTION, metricRegistry.tags(execution))
   214	                .increment();
   215	
   216	            logService.logExecution(
   217	                execution,
   218	                Level.INFO,
   219	                "Flow started"
   220	            );
   221	
   222	            newExecution = newExecution.withState(State.Type.RUNNING);
   223	        }
   224	
   225	        return newExecution;
   226	    }

   228	    private Optional<WorkerTaskResult> childWorkerTaskResult(Flow flow, Execution execution, TaskRun parentTaskRun) throws InternalException {
   229	        Task parent = flow.findTaskByTaskId(parentTaskRun.getTaskId());
   230	
   231	        if (parent instanceof FlowableTask<?> flowableParent) {
   232	
   233	            RunContext runContext = runContextFactory.of(flow, parent, execution, parentTaskRun);
   234	
   235	            // first find the normal ended child tasks and send result
   236	            Optional<State.Type> state;
   237	            try {
   238	                state = flowableParent.resolveState(runContext, execution, parentTaskRun);
   239	            } catch (Exception e) {
   240	                // This will lead to the next task being still executed but at least Kestra will not crash.
   241	                // This is the best we can do, Flowable task should not fail, so it's a kind of panic mode.
   242	                runContext.logger().error("Unable to resolve state from the Flowable task: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   243	                state = Optional.of(State.Type.FAILED);
   244	            }
   245	            Optional<WorkerTaskResult> endedTask = childWorkerTaskTypeToWorkerTask(
   246	                state,
   247	                parentTaskRun
   248	            );
   249	
   250	            if (endedTask.isPresent()) {
   251	                WorkerTaskResult workerTaskResult = endedTask.get();
   252	                // Compute outputs for the parent Flowable task if a terminated state was resolved
   253	                if (workerTaskResult.getTaskRun().getState().isTerminated()) {
   254	                    try {
   255	                        // as flowable tasks can save outputs during iterative execution, we must merge the maps here
   256	                        Output outputs = flowableParent.outputs(runContext);
   257	                        Map<String, Object> outputMap = MapUtils.merge(workerTaskResult.getTaskRun().getOutputs(), outputs == null ? null : outputs.toMap());
   258	                        Variables variables = variablesService.of(StorageContext.forTask(workerTaskResult.getTaskRun()), outputMap);
   259	                        return Optional.of(new WorkerTaskResult(workerTaskResult
   260	                            .getTaskRun()
   261	                            .withOutputs(variables)
   262	                        ));
   263	                    } catch (Exception e) {
   264	                        runContext.logger().error("Unable to resolve outputs from the Flowable task: {}", e.getMessage(), e);
   265	                    }
   266	                }
   267	                return endedTask;
   268	            }
   269	
   270	            // after if the execution is KILLING, we find if all already started tasks if finished
   271	            if (execution.getState().getCurrent() == State.Type.KILLING) {
   272	                // first notified the parent taskRun of killing to avoid new creation of tasks
   273	                if (parentTaskRun.getState().getCurrent() != State.Type.KILLING) {
   274	                    return childWorkerTaskTypeToWorkerTask(
   275	                        Optional.of(State.Type.KILLING),
   276	                        parentTaskRun
   277	                    );
   278	                }
   279	
   280	                // Then wait for completion (KILLED or whatever) on child tasks to KILLED the parent one.
   281	                List<ResolvedTask> currentTasks = execution.findTaskDependingFlowState(
   282	                    flowableParent.childTasks(runContext, parentTaskRun),
   283	                    FlowableUtils.resolveTasks(flowableParent.getErrors(), parentTaskRun),
   284	                    FlowableUtils.resolveTasks(flowableParent.getFinally(), parentTaskRun)
   285	                );
   286	
   287	                List<TaskRun> taskRunByTasks = execution.findTaskRunByTasks(currentTasks, parentTaskRun);
   288	
   289	                if (taskRunByTasks.stream().filter(t -> t.getState().isTerminated()).count() == taskRunByTasks.size()) {
   290	                    return childWorkerTaskTypeToWorkerTask(
   291	                        Optional.of(State.Type.KILLED),
   292	                        parentTaskRun
   293	                    );
   294	                }
   295	            }
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        return Optional.empty();
   299	    }
   300	
   301	    private Optional<WorkerTaskResult> childWorkerTaskTypeToWorkerTask(
   302	        Optional<State.Type> findState,
   303	        TaskRun taskRun
   304	    ) {
   305	        return findState
   306	            .map(throwFunction(type -> new WorkerTaskResult(taskRun.withState(type))));
   307	    }
   308	
   309	    private List<TaskRun> childNextsTaskRun(Executor executor, TaskRun parentTaskRun) throws InternalException {
   310	        Task parent = executor.getFlow().findTaskByTaskId(parentTaskRun.getTaskId());
   311	
   312	        if (parent instanceof FlowableTask<?> flowableParent) {
   313	            // Count the number of flowable tasks executions, some flowable are being called multiple times,
   314	            // so this is not exactly the number of flowable taskruns but the number of times they are executed.
   315	            metricRegistry
   316	                .counter(MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_FLOWABLE_EXECUTION_COUNT, MetricRegistry.METRIC_EXECUTOR_FLOWABLE_EXECUTION_COUNT_DESCRIPTION, metricRegistry.tags(parent))
   317	                .increment();
   318	
   319	            try {
   320	                List<NextTaskRun> nexts = flowableParent.resolveNexts(
   321	                    runContextFactory.of(
   322	                        executor.getFlow(),
   323	                        parent,
   324	                        executor.getExecution(),
   325	                        parentTaskRun
   326	                    ),
   327	                    executor.getExecution(),
   328	                    parentTaskRun
   329	                );
   330	
   331	                if (!nexts.isEmpty()) {
   332	                    return saveFlowableOutput(nexts, executor);
   333	                }
   334	            } catch (Exception e) {
   335	                log.warn("Unable to resolve the next tasks to run", e);
   336	            }
   337	        }
   338	
   339	        return Collections.emptyList();
   340	    }
   341	
   342	    private List<TaskRun> saveFlowableOutput(
   343	        List<NextTaskRun> nextTaskRuns,
   344	        Executor executor
   345	    ) {
   346	        return nextTaskRuns
   347	            .stream()
   348	            .map(throwFunction(t -> {
   349	                TaskRun taskRun = t.getTaskRun();
   350	
   351	                if (!(t.getTask() instanceof FlowableTask)) {
   352	                    return taskRun;
   353	                }
   354	                FlowableTask<?> flowableTask = (FlowableTask<?>) t.getTask();
   355	                RunContext runContext = runContextFactory.of(
   356	                    executor.getFlow(),
   357	                    t.getTask(),
   358	                    executor.getExecution(),
   359	                    t.getTaskRun()
   360	                );
   361	
   362	                try {
   363	                    Output outputs = flowableTask.outputs(runContext);
   364	                    Variables variables = variablesService.of(StorageContext.forTask(taskRun), outputs);
   365	                    taskRun = taskRun.withOutputs(variables);
   366	                } catch (Exception e) {
   367	                    runContext.logger().warn("Unable to save output on taskRun '{}'", taskRun, e);
   368	                }
   369	
   370	                return taskRun;
   371	            }))
   372	            .toList();
   373	    }

   945	        List<SubflowExecution<?>> executions = new ArrayList<>();
   946	        List<SubflowExecutionResult> subflowExecutionResults = new ArrayList<>();
   947	
   948	        boolean haveFlows = executor.getWorkerTasks()
   949	            .removeIf(workerTask -> {
   950	                if (!(workerTask.getTask() instanceof ExecutableTask)) {
   951	                    return false;
   952	                }
   953	
   954	                var executableTask = (Task & ExecutableTask<?>) workerTask.getTask();
   955	                try {
   956	                    // mark taskrun as running to avoid multiple try for failed
   957	                    TaskRun executableTaskRun = executor.getExecution()
   958	                        .findTaskRunByTaskRunId(workerTask.getTaskRun().getId());
   959	                    executor.withExecution(
   960	                        executor
   961	                            .getExecution()
   962	                            .withTaskRun(executableTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING)),
   963	                        "handleExecutableTaskRunning"
   964	                    );
   965	
   966	                    // handle runIf
   967	                    if (!TruthUtils.isTruthy(workerTask.getRunContext().render(workerTask.getTask().getRunIf()))) {
   968	                        executor.withExecution(
   969	                            executor
   970	                                .getExecution()
   971	                                .withTaskRun(executableTaskRun.withState(State.Type.SKIPPED)),
   972	                            "handleExecutableTaskSkipped"
   973	                        );
   974	                        return false;
   975	                    }
   976	
   977	                    RunContext runContext = runContextFactory.of(
   978	                        executor.getFlow(),
   979	                        executableTask,
   980	                        executor.getExecution(),
   981	                        executableTaskRun
   982	                    );
   983	                    List<SubflowExecution<?>> subflowExecutions = executableTask.createSubflowExecutions(runContext, flowExecutorInterface(), executor.getFlow(), executor.getExecution(), executableTaskRun);
   984	                    if (subflowExecutions.isEmpty()) {
   985	                        // if no executions we move the task to SUCCESS immediately
   986	                        executor.withExecution(
   987	                            executor
   988	                                .getExecution()
   989	                                .withTaskRun(executableTaskRun.withState(State.Type.SUCCESS)),
   990	                            "handleExecutableTaskRunning.noExecution"
   991	                        );
   992	                    } else {
   993	                        executions.addAll(subflowExecutions);
   994	                        Optional<FlowInterface> flow = flowExecutorInterface.findByExecution(subflowExecutions.getFirst().getExecution());
   995	                        if (flow.isPresent()) {
   996	                            // add SubflowExecutionResults to notify parents

   998	                                Optional<SubflowExecutionResult> subflowExecutionResult = executableTask.createSubflowExecutionResult(
   999	                                    runContext,
  1000	                                    // if we didn't wait for the execution, we directly set the state to SUCCESS
  1001	                                    executableTask.waitForExecution() ? subflowExecution.getParentTaskRun() : subflowExecution.getParentTaskRun().withState(State.Type.SUCCESS),
  1002	                                    flow.get(),
  1003	                                    subflowExecution.getExecution()
  1004	                                );
  1005	                                subflowExecutionResult.ifPresent(subflowExecutionResults::add);
  1006	                            }
  1007	                        } else {
  1008	                            log.error("Unable to find flow for execution {}", subflowExecutions.getFirst().getExecution().getId());
  1009	                        }
  1010	                    }
  1011	                } catch (Exception e) {
  1012	                    try {
  1013	                        executor
  1014	                            .withExecution(executor.getExecution().withTaskRun(workerTask.getTaskRun().fail()), "handleExecutableTask")
  1015	                            .withException(e, "handleExecutableTask");
  1016	                    } catch (InternalException ex) {
  1017	                        log.error("Unable to fail the executable task.", ex);
  1018	                    }
  1019	                }
  1020	                return true;
  1021	            });

  1024	            return executor;
  1025	        }

  1028

  1030	            resultExecutor = executor.withSubflowExecutionResults(subflowExecutionResults, "handleExecutableTaskWorkerTaskResults");
  1031	        }
  1032	
  1033	        return resultExecutor;
  1034	    }

   445	        if (executor.getExecution().getTaskRunList() == null) {
   446	            return executor;
   447	        }

   706	    private Executor handleAfterExecution(Executor executor) {
   707	        if (!executor.getExecution().getState().isTerminated()) {
   708	            return executor;
   709	        }
   710	
   711	        // first, execute listeners
   712	        List<ResolvedTask> listenerResolvedTasks = conditionService.findValidListeners(executor.getFlow(), executor.getExecution());
   713	        List<TaskRun> listenerNexts = FlowableUtils.resolveSequentialNexts(executor.getExecution(), listenerResolvedTasks)
   714	            .stream()
   715	            .map(throwFunction(NextTaskRun::getTaskRun))
   716	            .toList();
   717	
   718	        if (!listenerNexts.isEmpty()) {
   719	            return executor.withTaskRun(listenerNexts, "handleListeners");
   720	        }
   721	
   722	        // then, check if all listener tasks are terminated
   723	        if (!listenerResolvedTasks.isEmpty() && !executor.getExecution().isTerminated(listenerResolvedTasks)) {
   724	            return executor;
   725	        }
   726	
   727	        // then, when no more listeners, execute afterExecution tasks
   728	        List<ResolvedTask> afterExecutionResolvedTasks = executionService.resolveAfterExecutionTasks(executor.getFlow());
   729	        List<TaskRun> afterExecutionNexts = FlowableUtils.resolveSequentialNexts(executor.getExecution(), afterExecutionResolvedTasks)
   730	            .stream()
   731	            .map(throwFunction(NextTaskRun::getTaskRun))
   732	            .map(taskRun -> taskRun.withForceExecution(true)) // forceExecution so it would be executed even if the execution is killed
   733	            .toList();
   734	        if (!afterExecutionNexts.isEmpty()) {
   735	            return executor.withTaskRun(afterExecutionNexts, "handleAfterExecution ");
   736	        }
   737	
   738	        // if nothing more, just return the executor as is
   739	        return executor;
   740	    }
   741

   744	            return executor;
   745	        }

   748	            ResolvedTask.of(executor.getFlow().getTasks()),

        // first, execute listeners
        List<ResolvedTask> listenerResolvedTasks = conditionService.findValidListeners(executor.getFlow(), executor.getExecution());
        List<TaskRun> listenerNexts = FlowableUtils.resolveSequentialNexts(executor.getExecution(), listenerResolvedTasks)
            .stream()
            .map(throwFunction(NextTaskRun::getTaskRun))
            .toList();

        if (!listenerNexts.isEmpty()) {
            return executor.withTaskRun(listenerNexts, "handleListeners");
        }

        // then, check if all listener tasks are terminated
        if (!listenerResolvedTasks.isEmpty() && !executor.getExecution().isTerminated(listenerResolvedTasks)) {
            return executor;
        }

        // then, when no more listeners, execute afterExecution tasks
        List<ResolvedTask> afterExecutionResolvedTasks = executionService.resolveAfterExecutionTasks(executor.getFlow());
        List<TaskRun> afterExecutionNexts = FlowableUtils.resolveSequentialNexts(executor.getExecution(), afterExecutionResolvedTasks)
            .stream()
            .map(throwFunction(NextTaskRun::getTaskRun))
            .map(taskRun -> taskRun.withForceExecution(true)) // forceExecution so it would be executed even if the execution is killed
            .toList();
        if (!afterExecutionNexts.isEmpty()) {
            return executor.withTaskRun(afterExecutionNexts, "handleAfterExecution ");
        }

        // if nothing more, and afterExecution is actually finished
        if (!afterExecutionResolvedTasks.isEmpty() && !executor.getExecution().isTerminated(afterExecutionResolvedTasks)) {
            return executor;
        }

        // if nothing more, just return the executor as is
        return executor;
    }
'

    49	    public static State.Type guessState(Execution execution, boolean transmitFailed, boolean allowedFailure, boolean allowWarning) {
    50	        if (transmitFailed &&
    51	            (execution.getState().isFailed() || execution.getState().isPaused() || execution.getState().getCurrent() == State.Type.KILLED || execution.getState().getCurrent() == State.Type.WARNING)
    52	        ) {

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/core/src/main/java/io/kestra/core/runners/ExecutableUtils.java   --old_str '    public static <T extends Task & ExecutableTask<?>> Optional<SubflowExecution<?>> subflowExecution(
        RunContext runContext,
        FlowMetaStoreInterface flowExecutorInterface,
        Execution currentExecution,
        Flow currentFlow,
        T currentTask,
        TaskRun currentTaskRun,
        Map<String, Object> inputs,
        List<Label> labels,
        boolean inheritLabels,
        Property<ZonedDateTime> scheduleDate
    ) throws IllegalVariableEvaluationException {

        // extract a trace context for propagation
        final Optional<TextMapPropagator> propagator = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext()
            .findBean(OpenTelemetry.class)
            .map(OpenTelemetry::getPropagators)
            .map(ContextPropagators::getTextMapPropagator);

        var tracerFactory = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(TracerFactory.class);
        var tracer = tracerFactory.getTracer(currentTask.getClass(), "EXECUTOR");

        return tracer.inNewContext(
            currentExecution,
            currentTask.getType(),
            throwCallable(() -> {
            // If we are in a flow that is restarted, we search for existing run of the task to restart them
            if (currentExecution.getLabels() != null && currentExecution.getLabels().contains(new Label(Label.RESTARTED, "true"))
                && currentTask.getRestartBehavior() == ExecutableTask.RestartBehavior.RETRY_FAILED) {
                ExecutionRepositoryInterface executionRepository = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(ExecutionRepositoryInterface.class);

                Optional<Execution> existingSubflowExecution = Optional.empty();
                if (currentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null && currentTaskRun.getOutputs().containsKey("executionId")) {
                    // we know which execution to restart; this should be the case for Subflow tasks
                    existingSubflowExecution = executionRepository.findById(currentExecution.getTenantId(), (String) currentTaskRun.getOutputs().get("executionId"));
                }

                if (existingSubflowExecution.isEmpty()) {
                    // otherwise, we try to find the correct one; this should be the case for ForEachItem tasks
                    List<Execution> childExecutions = executionRepository.findAllByTriggerExecutionId(currentExecution.getTenantId(), currentExecution.getId())
                        .filter(e -> e.getNamespace().equals(currentTask.subflowId().namespace()) && e.getFlowId().equals(currentTask.subflowId().flowId()) && e.getTrigger().getId().equals(currentTask.getId()))
                        .filter(e -> Objects.equals(e.getTrigger().getVariables().get("taskRunId"), currentTaskRun.getId()) && Objects.equals(e.getTrigger().getVariables().get("taskRunValue"), currentTaskRun.getValue()) && Objects.equals(e.getTrigger().getVariables().get("taskRunIteration"), currentTaskRun.getIteration()))
                        .collectList()
                        .block();

                    if (childExecutions != null && childExecutions.size() == 1) {
                        // if there are more than one, we ignore the results and create a new one
                        existingSubflowExecution = Optional.of(childExecutions.getFirst());
                    }
                }

                if (existingSubflowExecution.isPresent()) {
                    Execution subflowExecution = existingSubflowExecution.get();
                    if (!subflowExecution.getState().isFailed()) {
                        // don'"'"'t restart it as it'"'"'s terminated successfully
                        return Optional.empty();
                    }
                    ExecutionService executionService = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(ExecutionService.class);
                    try {
                        Execution restarted = executionService.restart(subflowExecution, null);

                        // inject the traceparent into the new execution
                        propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), restarted, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));

                        return Optional.of(SubflowExecution.builder()
                            .parentTask(currentTask)
                            .parentTaskRun(currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING))
                            .execution(restarted)
                            .build());
                    } catch (Exception e) {
                        throw new RuntimeException(e);
                    }
                }
            }

            String subflowNamespace = runContext.render(currentTask.subflowId().namespace());
            String subflowId = runContext.render(currentTask.subflowId().flowId());
            Optional<Integer> subflowRevision = currentTask.subflowId().revision();

            FlowInterface flow = flowExecutorInterface.findByIdFromTask(
                    currentExecution.getTenantId(),
                    subflowNamespace,
                    subflowId,
                    subflowRevision,
                    currentExecution.getTenantId(),
                    currentFlow.getNamespace(),
                    currentFlow.getId()
                )
                .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Unable to find flow '"'"'" + subflowNamespace + "'"'"'.'"'"'" + subflowId + "'"'"' with revision '"'"'" + subflowRevision.orElse(0) + "'"'"'"));

            if (flow.isDisabled()) {
                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot execute a flow which is disabled");
            }

            if (flow instanceof FlowWithException fwe) {
                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot execute an invalid flow: " + fwe.getException());
            }

            List<Label> newLabels = inheritLabels ? new ArrayList<>(filterLabels(currentExecution.getLabels(), flow)) : new ArrayList<>(systemLabels(currentExecution));
            if (labels != null) {
                labels.forEach(throwConsumer(label -> newLabels.add(new Label(runContext.render(label.key()), runContext.render(label.value())))));
            }

            var variables = ImmutableMap.<String, Object>builder().putAll(Map.of(
                "executionId", currentExecution.getId(),
                "namespace", currentFlow.getNamespace(),
                "flowId", currentFlow.getId(),
                "flowRevision", currentFlow.getRevision(),
                "taskRunId", currentTaskRun.getId(),
                "taskId", currentTaskRun.getTaskId()
            ));
            if (currentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null) {
                variables.put("taskRunOutputs", currentTaskRun.getOutputs());
            }
            if (currentTaskRun.getValue() != null) {
                variables.put("taskRunValue", currentTaskRun.getValue());
            }
            if (currentTaskRun.getIteration() != null) {
                variables.put("taskRunIteration", currentTaskRun.getIteration());
            }

            FlowInputOutput flowInputOutput = ((DefaultRunContext)runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(FlowInputOutput.class);
            Instant scheduleOnDate = runContext.render(scheduleDate).as(ZonedDateTime.class).map(date -> date.toInstant()).orElse(null);
            Execution execution = Execution
                .newExecution(
                    flow,
                    (f, e) -> flowInputOutput.readExecutionInputs(f, e, inputs),
                    newLabels,
                    Optional.empty())
                .withTrigger(ExecutionTrigger.builder()
                    .id(currentTask.getId())
                    .type(currentTask.getType())
                    .variables(variables.build())
                    .build()
                )
                .withScheduleDate(scheduleOnDate);

            // inject the traceparent into the new execution
            propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), execution, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));

            return Optional.of(SubflowExecution.builder()
                .parentTask(currentTask)
                .parentTaskRun(currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING))
                .execution(execution)
                .build());
        }));
    }

        Map<String, Object> inputs,
        List<Label> labels,
        boolean inheritLabels,
        Property<ZonedDateTime> scheduleDate
    ) throws IllegalVariableEvaluationException {

        // extract a trace context for propagation
        final Optional<TextMapPropagator> propagator = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext()
            .findBean(OpenTelemetry.class)
            .map(OpenTelemetry::getPropagators)
            .map(ContextPropagators::getTextMapPropagator);

        var tracerFactory = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(TracerFactory.class);
        var tracer = tracerFactory.getTracer(currentTask.getClass(), "EXECUTOR");

        return tracer.inNewContext(
            currentExecution,
            currentTask.getType(),
            throwCallable(() -> {
            // If we are in a flow that is restarted, we search for existing run of the task to restart them
            if (currentExecution.getLabels() != null && currentExecution.getLabels().contains(new Label(Label.RESTARTED, "true"))
                && currentTask.getRestartBehavior() == ExecutableTask.RestartBehavior.RETRY_FAILED) {
                ExecutionRepositoryInterface executionRepository = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(ExecutionRepositoryInterface.class);

                Optional<Execution> existingSubflowExecution = Optional.empty();

                    existingSubflowExecution = executionRepository.findById(currentExecution.getTenantId(), (String) currentTaskRun.getOutputs().get("executionId"));
                }

                if (existingSubflowExecution.isEmpty()) {
                    // otherwise, we try to find the correct one; this should be the case for ForEachItem tasks
                    List<Execution> childExecutions = executionRepository.findAllByTriggerExecutionId(currentExecution.getTenantId(), currentExecution.getId())

                        .collectList()
                        .block();

                    if (childExecutions != null && childExecutions.size() == 1) {
                        // if there are more than one, we ignore the results and create a new one
                        existingSubflowExecution = Optional.of(childExecutions.getFirst());
                    }
                }

                    Execution subflowExecution = existingSubflowExecution.get();
                    if (!subflowExecution.getState().isFailed()) {
                        // don'"'"'t restart it as it'"'"'s terminated successfully
                        return Optional.empty();

                    ExecutionService executionService = ((DefaultRunContext) runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(ExecutionService.class);

                        Execution restarted = executionService.restart(subflowExecution, null);

                        // inject the traceparent into the new execution
                        propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), restarted, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));

                            .parentTaskRun(currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING))

                            .build());
                    } catch (Exception e) {
                        throw new RuntimeException(e);
                    }
                }
            }

            String subflowNamespace = runContext.render(currentTask.subflowId().namespace());
            String subflowId = runContext.render(currentTask.subflowId().flowId());
            Optional<Integer> subflowRevision = currentTask.subflowId().revision();

            FlowInterface flow = flowExecutorInterface.findByIdFromTask(
                    currentExecution.getTenantId(),
                    subflowNamespace,
                    subflowId,
                    subflowRevision,
                    currentExecution.getTenantId(),
                    currentFlow.getNamespace(),
                    currentFlow.getId()
                )
                .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Unable to find flow '"'"'" + subflowNamespace + "'"'"'.'"'"'" + subflowId + "'"'"' with revision '"'"'" + subflowRevision.orElse(0) + "'"'"'"));

            if (flow.isDisabled()) {
                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot execute a flow which is disabled");
            }

            if (flow instanceof FlowWithException fwe) {
                throw new IllegalStateException("Cannot execute an invalid flow: " + fwe.getException());
            }

            List<Label> newLabels = inheritLabels ? new ArrayList<>(filterLabels(currentExecution.getLabels(), flow)) : new ArrayList<>(systemLabels(currentExecution));
            if (labels != null) {
                labels.forEach(throwConsumer(label -> newLabels.add(new Label(runContext.render(label.key()), runContext.render(label.value())))));
            }

            var variables = ImmutableMap.<String, Object>builder().putAll(Map.of(
                "executionId", currentExecution.getId(),
                "namespace", currentFlow.getNamespace(),
                "flowId", currentFlow.getId(),
                "flowRevision", currentFlow.getRevision(),
                "taskRunId", currentTaskRun.getId(),
                "taskId", currentTaskRun.getTaskId()
            ));
            if (currentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null) {
                variables.put("taskRunOutputs", currentTaskRun.getOutputs());
            }
            if (currentTaskRun.getValue() != null) {
                variables.put("taskRunValue", currentTaskRun.getValue());
            }
            if (currentTaskRun.getIteration() != null) {
                variables.put("taskRunIteration", currentTaskRun.getIteration());
            }

            FlowInputOutput flowInputOutput = ((DefaultRunContext)runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(FlowInputOutput.class);
            Instant scheduleOnDate = runContext.render(scheduleDate).as(ZonedDateTime.class).map(date -> date.toInstant()).orElse(null);
            Execution execution = Execution
                .newExecution(
                    flow,
                    (f, e) -> flowInputOutput.readExecutionInputs(f, e, inputs),
                    newLabels,
                    Optional.empty())
                .withTrigger(ExecutionTrigger.builder()
                    .id(currentTask.getId())
                    .type(currentTask.getType())
                    .variables(variables.build())
                    .build()
                )
                .withScheduleDate(scheduleOnDate);

            // inject the traceparent into the new execution
            propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), execution, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));

            TaskRun parentTaskRun = currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING);
            if (flow.getAfterExecution() != null && !flow.getAfterExecution().isEmpty()) {
                Map<String, Object> outputs = parentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null ? new HashMap<>(parentTaskRun.getOutputs()) : new HashMap<>();
                outputs.put(TASK_VARIABLE_SUBFLOW_AFTER_EXECUTION, true);
                parentTaskRun = parentTaskRun.withOutputs(outputs);
            }

            return Optional.of(SubflowExecution.builder()
                .parentTask(currentTask)
                .parentTaskRun(parentTaskRun)
                .execution(execution)
                .build());
        }));
    }

   188	                variables.put("taskRunIteration", currentTaskRun.getIteration());
   189	            }
   190	
   191	            FlowInputOutput flowInputOutput = ((DefaultRunContext)runContext).getApplicationContext().getBean(FlowInputOutput.class);
   192	            Instant scheduleOnDate = runContext.render(scheduleDate).as(ZonedDateTime.class).map(date -> date.toInstant()).orElse(null);
   193	            Execution execution = Execution
   194	                .newExecution(
   195	                    flow,
   196	                    (f, e) -> flowInputOutput.readExecutionInputs(f, e, inputs),
   197	                    newLabels,
   198	                    Optional.empty())
   199	                .withTrigger(ExecutionTrigger.builder()
   200	                    .id(currentTask.getId())
   201	                    .type(currentTask.getType())
   202	                    .variables(variables.build())
   203	                    .build()
   204	                )
   205	                .withScheduleDate(scheduleOnDate);
   206	
   207	            // inject the traceparent into the new execution
   208	            propagator.ifPresent(pg -> pg.inject(Context.current(), execution, ExecutionTextMapSetter.INSTANCE));
   209	
   210	            TaskRun parentTaskRun = currentTaskRun.withState(State.Type.RUNNING);
   211	            if (flow.getAfterExecution() != null && !flow.getAfterExecution().isEmpty()) {
   212	                Map<String, Object> outputs = parentTaskRun.getOutputs() != null ? new HashMap<>(parentTaskRun.getOutputs()) : new HashMap<>();
   213	                outputs.put(TASK_VARIABLE_SUBFLOW_AFTER_EXECUTION, true);
   214	                parentTaskRun = parentTaskRun.withOutputs(outputs);
   215	            }
   216	
   217	            return Optional.of(SubflowExecution.builder()
   218	                .parentTask(currentTask)
   219	                .parentTaskRun(parentTaskRun)
   220	                .execution(execution)
   221	                .build());
   222	        }));
   223	    }

   226	        if (ListUtils.isEmpty(flow.getLabels())) {
   227	            return labels;
